# Get TrackedMessageEvent: application/json
## Get TrackedMessageEvent

  Response Content Type: **application/json**

Request
---
Response Class (Status 200)

OK

Method  | Request URL
------------- | -------------
GET  | http://biztalkfp1.westus.cloudapp.azure.com/BizTalkManagementService/OperationalData/TrackedMessageEvents

Response
---

| Response | Content          |
| ------------- | ----------- |
| Curl | curl -X GET --header 'Accept: application/json' 'http://biztalkfp1.westus.cloudapp.azure.com/BizTalkManagementService/OperationalData/TrackedMessageEvents'|
| Response Code | 200|
